 pratiraksha or vimaanan kii tonbo imaging company ke maalik 42 varshiya arvind lakshmikumar hai
 Tonbo Imaging is an OEM (original equipment manufacturer) with advanced imaging to create sensor systems that detect and control complex environments
 bits pilaani ke purv chaatr arvind lakshmikumar ne 2008 main isaki neenv rakhi thi
 It manufactures advanced imaging systems, night vision devices and thermal imagers

 Many government agencies including the Indian Army, Indian Air Force, BSF, National Security Guard and CRPF are its customers

 Tonbo caters to all requirements in line with market demand in the fields of military espionage, critical infrastructural security and transport security
 unnat imaging product custom dizin aplication or bauddhik sampada company kii asli takat hai

 Free wifi ke darjanon khatre hai
 Your smartphone can also be hacked
 free wifai yaa public wifai yuj karnaa aapke liye ek risk kii tarah he
 It is true that if public wifi is kept safe then the risk of hacking on end users is less, but in India, the system is weak about data and cyber security
 aise main agar aapako agar kahin free wifai yaa public wifai mil rahaa he to aapako ise yuj karne se pehle saavdhaan rahane kii jarurat he
 Because it has many serious dangers
 mote shabdon main kahen to aapkaa mobile phone main rakhaa samvedansheel data chori ho saktaa he
 By using free or public wifi, the login details saved on your mobile can be stolen
 aap havers ke nishane par aa sakate hai or aapke smartphone ke saath ched chhaad kiya ja saktaa he
 Arvind Kejriwal government has announced the installation of free wifi hot spots in Delhi
 jald hi bas stand par or duusare public place par aaf free wifai yuj kar paaenge
 Users will be given 15GB of data every month
 kitna sicyor hote hai public wifipublic wifai yuj karne ke saikadon risk hai
 Before this you will need to know how public wifi work
 jagah jagah par wifai hot spot lagaae jaaenge
 How secure the hot spots will be installed by the Delhi government will be known in the coming times
 kyonki jab ye test nahin kiya jaae ki in wifai hot spot ke liye koun sa ancripshan system yuj kiya ja rahaa he, ye kahana mushkil he ki ye aapke liye sicyor he yaa nahin
 However, the biggest disadvantage of running internet in your mobile or laptop by connecting to free or public wifi is that your data can be stolen
 ab aap soch rahe honge ye kaise sambhav he?main in da middle atex ke jariye havers public wifai se jude smartphone or laptops aasaani se hack kar sakate hai
 The data travel that takes place in the connection between your mobile and the hot spot is in packet form
 havers ise kai tuls kaa sahaara lekar chori karte hai
 Although this data is encrypted, it can still be decrypted
 aap kisi email karenge, kol karenge, photo share karenge or is tarah kii tamaam activity ko haikar aaraam se colect kar saktaa he
 The most serious is that if you are doing any transaction through public wifi or free wifi, then your card details can also be stolen
 public wifai ke jariye havers aapke smartphone main aasaani se mailaware inject kar sakate hai
 After this, sensitive information can be stolen by remotely controlling your smartphone
 ek khaas tarah ke software ke jariye wifai signlles kii bhi jasusi kii jaati he
 Through this, the hacker can monitor real-time the activity of your smartphone or laptop
 ise snifing bhi kah sakate hai
 Most cyber security firms and experts recommend that using public wifi should be avoided
 iske baavjood bhi kuch aise tareeken hai jin par amal karke aap public wifai conect karne ke baad bhi sicyor rah sakate hai

 sudeep, pradesh kisatnavidhansabha seat se nirdaleey chunaav lard rahe hai
 aajtak
 inne sudeep ke interprator gyanendra purohit se baat kii

 africa main 2 or nepal-newjiland main 1-1 mook-badhir ne chunaav ladaa he

 unhen, sudeep kii jeet kaa bhi bharosa he or iske peeche unke apane tark hai
 Gyanendra says the land of Vindhya has always been with change
 yahaan ke jatigat sameekaran savarna or obisi aadhaarit hai

 sudeep satna se hi aate hai or unke dada congress kii raajnneeti main sakriy rahe hai

 The rate contract has become a weapon of new political battle in Maharashtra
 bijepi banaam congress kii raajnneetik ladaai main ise aajkal khub istemaal kiya ja rahaa he
 a rate contract is a government document on the basis of which the government purchases the goods required for it
 is contract se saamaan kisase or kis daam par kharida jaae yah tay hota he
 Maharashtra Congress had recently alleged that Pankaja Munde, the Minister of Women and Child Welfare in the BJP government of the state, purchased goods worth Rs 206 crore by resorting to rate contracts
 congress kah rahi he kii yah niyamon kaa ulanghan he
 Now it is bjp's turn
 vah isi rate contract kaa sahaara le kar congress ko gherne kii ranneeti taiyaar kar chuki he
 The state government has initiated an inquiry into all the purchases made through rate contracts in the last ten years
 taaki is main hui aniyamitataayen ujagar ho saken
 Maharashtra Finance Minister Sudhir Munghantiwar told NDTV India that the investigation has started on receiving information about non-supply of goods despite payment from the government
 rajya ke 4 hajaar godown main aniyamit aapurti kii ashanka se is jaanch ko bal mila he
 It is to be known that the rate contracts are under the state Department of Industries
 pichley das saal tak in mahakamon kaa jimmaa pehle ashok chavaan or phir narayan rane in congressi netaaon ke paas tha
 The statement of BJP Minister Pankaja Munde has been the reason for the background of this investigation
 shrimati munde lagaataar kah rahi hai ki unke kaarykaal main keval 206 karod rupee kii kharidi hui jise ghotaalaa kaha gaya
 However, during the last 5 years of the Congress, Rs 408 crore has been purchased which should be investigated
 tippaniyan By the way, the work of giving air to this investigation is also seen from inside the Congress
 rajya main gat das saal kii congress ensipi shasankaal main lambe vakt tak siem rahe prithviraj chavaan is jaanch ko samarthan de rahe hai

 Rakesh Asthana, Additional Director, Gujarat Cadre, has been made Special Director in CBI
 IPS afasar rakesh asthana vahi hai, jinhen bahucharchit chaara ghotaale kii jaanch kii jimmedaari di gai thi
 He filed a charge sheet against Lalu Yadav in 1996 and got him arrested
 rakesh asthana kaa janm 1961 main ranchi main hua tha
 He got his initial education from Netarhat School in Jharkhand
 inke pita echaar asthana netarhat skool main bhautikee ke shikshak the
 After this, he studied at St
 Xavier's College, Ranchi
 1978 main aiessi karne ke baad agra sthit apane paitruk ghar chale gaye
 After getting higher education from Jawaharlal Nehru University, Delhi, he started teaching history at St
 Xavier's College, Ranchi
 1984 main unhone apane pehle hi prayaas main upiessi kii pariksha paas kar lee or ipies adhikari ban gaye
 He got Gujarat cadre
 vah dhanbad main sibiai kii bhrashtachar nirodhak shakha ke espi rah chuke hai
 He was in the rank of DIG in Ranchi
 rakesh asthana kaa naam kartavyanishth or eemaandaar adhikariyon kii suchi main khaas taur se shaamil rahaa he
 In 1994, he supervised the field investigation of the sensational Purulia Arms Drop Case
 unhen bahucharchit chaara ghotaale kii jaanch kii jimmedaari di gai
 He filed a chargesheet against Lalu Prasad Yadav in 1996
 1997 main unke samay hi lalu pehali baar giraftaar hue
 He was 35 at the time
 wo tab sibiai espi ke taur par tainaat the
 Asthana is originally known only for questioning Lalu
 1997 ko unhone chaara ghotaale main lalu se 6 ghante tak poochtacha kii thi
 It was Asthana who caught the Director General of DGMS taking a bribe in Dhanbad
 us samay tak puure desh main apane tareeke kaa yah pehla maamla tha, jab mahanideshak str ke adhikari sibiai giraft main aaye the
